When `Exited()` returns true, indicating the process has crashed, `keepPluginAlive()` calls `p.Start()` to restart the plugin. It defines the `HandshakeConfig` with protocol version and magic cookie validation, and supports both process mode and container mode execution.\\n- `pkg/plugins/backendplugin/grpcplugin/grpc_plugin.go` contains the `grpcPlugin` struct that manages the plugin client lifecycle. It calls `plugin.NewClient()` from hashicorp/go-plugin to establish the connection.\\n- `pkg/plugins/backendplugin/grpcplugin/client_v2.go` implements `ClientV2` which wraps the gRPC clients for all supported plugin interfaces (Diagnostics, Resource, Data, Stream, Admission, Conversion).\\n\\n**Plugin Health Check**: Health checking is implemented at multiple levels:\\n- `pkg/plugins/backendplugin/grpcplugin/client_v2.go` implements the `CheckHealth()` method that calls the `DiagnosticsClient.CheckHealth()` gRPC endpoint, handling protocol-specific error codes.\\n- `pkg/plugins/manager/client/client.go` contains the `Service` type with a `CheckHealth()` method that retrieves plugins from the registry and delegates to their `CheckHealth()` method.\\n- `pkg/plugins/plugins.go` wraps backend plugins through the `Plugin` struct, delegating `CheckHealth()` calls to the underlying `client` (backendplugin.Plugin).\\n\\n**Plugin Restart Policy**: The restart logic is in `pkg/plugins/manager/process/process.go`'s `keepPluginAlive()` function. It continuously monitors the plugin using `p.Exited()`, which is implemented in `pkg/plugins/backendplugin/grpcplugin/grpc_plugin.go`. When `Exited()` returns true, indicating the process has crashed, `keepPluginAlive()` calls `p.Start()` to restart the plugin. The function only exits when the plugin is explicitly decommissioned via `p.IsDecommissioned()`.\\n\\n**Plugin State Management**: `pkg/plugins/backendplugin/grpcplugin/grpc_plugin.go` tracks plugin state using a `pluginState` enum (NotStarted, StartInit, StartSuccess, StartFail, Stopped). The `grpcPlugin` struct maintains synchronization with mutex locks and provides thread-safe access to the plugin client through `getPluginClient()`.\\n\\n**Plugin Lifecycle Initialization**: `pkg/plugins/manager/pipeline/initialization/steps.go` implements `BackendClientInit` for creating the plugin client and `BackendClientStarter` for starting the process. The termination counterpart is in `pkg/plugins/manager/pipeline/termination/steps.go` with `BackendProcessTerminator`. Core plugins are handled separately in `pkg/plugins/backendplugin/coreplugin/core_plugin.go` which implements plugins that are built into Grafana itself.\"\n}\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}
